 ’ How well you drive is a reflection of how quickly and how well you park the car
 yakeenan ek achche driver kii yahi pahchaan he, lekin vyast sadakon or parking aria main car ko khadi karne se pehle hamen kuch saavdhaaniyon par dhyaan dene kii bhi jarurat he
 1) Before parking the car, please check whether the place is for parking or not
 2)no standing jone, no parking jone kaa khaas khyal rakhen
 3) Never park the car in front of a gate
 4)bas stop, post box, taxi yaa rickshaw stand jaise bheed vaale ilaakon main bhi gaadi park karne se bachein
 5) It is better not to park the car under any tree
 6)ped ke neeche gaadi park karne se din ke samay aapaki gaadi dhoop se to batch sakati he, lekin tahaniyon ke girane yaa aandhi-tufaan kii sthiti main ped ke girane par zyada nuksaan uthaanaa pad saktaa he
 7) By storing the car under the tree, the feces of the birds can also spoil the paint of your car
 8)hand brake ke istemaal kaa sahi tarika seekhen
 9) Generally people park the car and put it in gear and apply hand brake
 aisa nahin karen
 The maximum load in such a situation is on the gear and not the hand brake
 10)pahari ilaakon main car park karte vakt hand brake kaa istemaal jarur karen
 11) If you want to park the car near the garden, then definitely apply hand brake
 12)behatar hoga gaadi ko neutral giyar main daalkar hand brake lagaaein
 13) While using the hand brake, press its push button
 14)diwaar ke bagal main gaadi khadi kar rahe hai to diwaar se thodi duuri banaakar rakhen
 15) Do not block any road while parking the car

 The Goods and Services Tax has come into force from 1 July
 is nai tex pranali main kai aise praavdhaan jise jaankaar maan rahe hai ki inke chalate desh main ek baar inspector raaj kii shuruyaat ho sakati he
 The GST law is supposed to provide for the arrest of a businessman for profits and tax inconsistency, which will give the tax department employees exclusive powers to inspect, raid and confiscate the business locations
 in praavdhaanon se desh main kaarobaariyon ke liye tex vibhaag ke field afasar ko aseem shaktiyaan mil jaaengi
 CGST and SGSTK employees can conduct inspections and raids on any business or transporter or warehouse merely on the suspicion that the said tax is being or is likely to be stolen
 vahiin jiesti main cloj 171 main praavdhaan kiya gaya he ki companiyon ko input tex credit se milane vaala phayda graahakon ko saste utpaada uplabdh karakar dena hoga
 Under this rule, it is necessary to set up a structure parallel to the GST structure, so that the profitability of companies can be closely monitored
 iske alaava, jiesti ke praavdhaanon par tex maamalon ke jaankaron kaa maananaa he ki tex kii daren 5,12, 18 or 28 fisadi ke chalate kaarobaari or tex vibhaag ke bich kai nae matbhed paidaa ho sakate hai

 Most of the people, male or female, sit with their legs crossed
 isaki ek vajah yah he ki is posture ko kaaphi stylish mana jaataa he
 If you also have a habit of sitting with your legs crossed, then be careful
 kyonki kai health export ne pairon ko cross karke baithne kii aadat ko sehat liye kaaphi khatarnaak bataaya he
 Actually, this style of your sitting can make you a victim of many diseases
 isliye baithte samay is baat kaa jarur dhyaan rakhen ki aap zyada samay tak kisi ek posture main naa baithe
 To keep healthy, change your posture from time to time
 aaie jaanate hai pairon ko cross karke baithne se hone vaali bimaariyaan
 
 
 1
 blad pressure kaa badhanaa:kai studies main yah baat sabit ho chuki he ki zyada samay tak pairon ko cross karke baithne sebled pressure kaaphi had tak bad jaataa he
 Therefore, health experts instruct people with blood pressure victims to avoid sitting in this posture who do not have trouble with blood pressure
 2
 Risk of nerve paralysis: If you sit with your legs crossed for too long, it can damage the nerves of your feet
 kyonki aise baithne par pairon kii nason par pressure bad jaataa he jis vajah se nason ke dames hone kaa khatra rahata he
 Not only this, but sitting in this posture can also be a victim of person pararenol nerve paralysis
 3
 Increased blood circulation: Due to sitting with one leg on the other leg, more blood reaches the heart
 kyonki jab aap pairon ko cross karke baithte hai to blad upar se neeche kii taraf aana band kar detaa he orheart ulta pump karnaa shuru kar detaa he
 Because of which the blood circulation in the body gets disturbed
 4
 Danger of Spider Vein: By keeping one leg on the other for long time, you can fall prey to Spider Vein
 kyonki ek pair ko duusare pair par rakhkar baithne se pairon main pahunchane vaala khun ruk kar waapas dil main hi sarculate ho jaataa he
